<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Moon_Studio/Mid-Autumn/2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants:</b>
<ul><li>Eighteen invited teams</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>October 1st - October 19th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>One group of Southeast Asian teams, one group of China teams</li>
<li>Single round-robin</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-two">Bo2</abbr></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">Top team</span> from each group advance to the Upper Bracket R2 of the Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(229,244,198);">2<sup>nd</sup> and 3<sup>rd</sup> place teams</span> from each group advance to the Upper Bracket R1 of the Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(249,240,199);">4<sup>th</sup> place teams</span> from each group advance to the Lower Bracket R2 of the Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(249,222,199);">5<sup>th</sup> and 6<sup>th</sup> place teams</span> from each group advance to the Lower Bracket R1 of the Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Remaining teams</span> from each group are eliminated</li>
<li><span class="mw-customtoggle-Tiebreaker" style="border-bottom:1px dotted;"><i>Click here for tiebreaker rules</i></span></li></ul></li></ul>
<div class="toccolours mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" id="mw-customcollapsible-Tiebreaker" style="width:760px; margin-left:45px">
<ol><li>Number of matches won 2:0</li>
<li>Head-to-head result</li>
<li>In the case that the above process cannot break a tie, <abbr title="Best-of-one">Bo1</abbr> tiebreaker will be played</li></ol>
</div>
<ul><li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>October 23rd - October 28th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>, all other matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
